# 🚨 ENHANCED SHELL PATTERNS
REAL_THREATS = [
    r'eval\s*\(base64_decode',r'base64_decode\s*\(\$|base64_decode\s*\(\$_?POST',
    r'gzinflate',r'exec|system|passthru|shell_exec',r'assert\s*\(\$',
    r'move_uploaded_file\s*\(\$_',r'\$_POST\["cmd"|pass|exec',r'c99|wso|indoxploit',
    r'\\x62\\x61\\x73\\x64',r'adminer\(\)|phpmyadmin',r'preg_replace\s*/\/e/',
    r'create_function|gzdecode|gzuncompress',r'\$_GET\["cmd"|exec|shell',
    r'\.dat["\']|\.datfile',r'SetHandler\s*application/x-httpd-php'
]

# 🔒 GLOBAL LOCK & STORAGE
shells_lock = threading.Lock()
checked_lock = threading.Lock()
all_shells = []
domain_shells = {}

def send_telegram_alert(message):
    try:
        url = f"https://api.telegram.org/bot{TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN}/sendMessage"
        data = {"chat_id": TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID, "text": message, "parse_mode": "HTML"}
        requests.post(url, data=data, timeout=5)
        print("📱 Telegram OK!")
    except: print("⚠️ Telegram failed")

def load_domains():
    if not os.path.exists(DOMAIN_FILE):
        print(f"❌ {DOMAIN_FILE} tidak ada!\nContoh:\nhttps://target1.com\nhttps://target2.com")
        sys.exit(1)
    return [l.strip() for l in open(DOMAIN_FILE) if l.strip() and not l.startswith('#')]

def banner():
    print("""
🔍 OJS v16.7 - ⚡ ULTRA FAST RECURSIVE + 25 THREADS + TELEGRAM!
✅ 37+ locales | Deep scan | No duplicates | Token built-in
✅ CUKUP: python scanner.py → LIGHTNING SCAN!
    """)

def analyze_php_file(full_url, base_url):
    rel_path = full_url.replace(base_url, '').lstrip('/')
    try:
        resp = requests.get(full_url, timeout=8, verify=False)
        content = resp.text.strip()
        size = len(content)
        print(f"({size}b)", end=" ")
        
        if size == 0: print("📄"); return False
        if size < 100: print("⚪")
        elif size < 1000: print("📄")
        else: print("📕")
        
        if resp.status_code != 200: 
            print(f"H{resp.status_code}"); return False
        
        lines = content.split('\n')[:2]  # 2 lines only for speed
        preview = ' | '.join(line.strip()[:30] for line in lines if line.strip())
        print(f"| {preview}")
        
        hits = []
        for pattern in REAL_THREATS:
            if re.search(pattern, content, re.IGNORECASE):
                m = re.search(pattern, content, re.IGNORECASE)
                hits.append(f"{pattern[:15]}→{m.group(0)[:25]}")
                if len(hits) >= 3: break  # Limit hits for speed
        
        if hits:
            print(f"\n🕵️ SHELL DETECTED!")
            for hit in hits[:2]: print(f"   → {hit}")
            print("-" * 40)
            
            alert_msg = f"""🚨<b>SHELL!</b> {base_url}/{rel_path}\n📍<a href="{full_url}">{full_url}</a>"""
            send_telegram_alert(alert_msg)
            return True
        print("🟢")
        return False
    except: print("❌"); return False

def is_subpath_under_listed(candidate_rel_path, listed_paths):
    for listed in listed_paths:
        if candidate_rel_path == listed or candidate_rel_path.startswith(listed):
            return True
    return False

def visit_path_recursive_threadsafe(base_url, base_full_url, base_rel_path, reviewed_paths, checked_urls, domain_shells):
    if not is_subpath_under_listed(base_rel_path, reviewed_paths): return
    
    with checked_lock:
        if base_full_url in checked_urls: return
        checked_urls.add(base_full_url)
    
    try:
        resp = requests.get(base_full_url, timeout=8, verify=False)
        if resp.status_code != 200: return
        
        soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, 'html.parser')
        
        for a in soup.find_all('a', href=True):
            href = a['href'].strip()
            if href in ['../', '/', '']: continue
            
            full_url = urljoin(base_full_url, href)
            rel_path = full_url.replace(base_url, '').lstrip('/')
            
            if not is_subpath_under_listed(rel_path, reviewed_paths): continue
            
            with checked_lock:
                if full_url in checked_urls: continue
                checked_urls.add(full_url)
            
            if href.endswith('/'):
                # ⚡ THREAD SUBFOLDERS (MAX DEPTH)
                if rel_path.count('/') < 5:  # Limit recursion depth
                    print(f"   📁 {rel_path}")
                    visit_path_recursive_threadsafe(base_url, full_url, rel_path, reviewed_paths, checked_urls, domain_shells)
            elif href.lower().endswith('.php'):
                print(f"   📄 {rel_path}", end=" ")
                if analyze_php_file(full_url, base_url):
                    with shells_lock:
                        domain_shells.setdefault(base_url, []).append(full_url)
        
        # Quick index.php check
        index_url = urljoin(base_full_url, 'index.php')
        index_rel = index_url.replace(base_url, '').lstrip('/')
        if (is_subpath_under_listed(index_rel, reviewed_paths) and 
            index_url not in checked_urls):
            with checked_lock:
                if index_url not in checked_urls:
                    checked_urls.add(index_url)
                    print(f"   🔍 {index_rel}", end=" ")
                    if analyze_php_file(index_url, base_url):
                        with shells_lock:
                            domain_shells.setdefault(base_url, []).append(index_url)
                            
    except: pass

def scan_initial_paths_threaded(base_url, reviewed_paths):
    """⚡ THREAD INITIAL PATHS (25 threads like v16.5)"""
    checked_urls = set()
    domain_shells = {}
    
    print(f"🎯 {base_url}")
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=25) as executor:
        futures = []
        for i, path in enumerate(reviewed_paths):
            base_full_url = urljoin(base_url.rstrip('/') + '/', path.lstrip('/'))
            rel_path = base_full_url.replace(base_url, '').lstrip('/')
            
            # Quick HEAD check first
            try:
                if requests.head(base_full_url, timeout=3, verify=False).status_code == 200:
                    future = executor.submit(visit_path_recursive_threadsafe, base_url, base_full_url, rel_path, reviewed_paths, checked_urls, domain_shells)
                    futures.append(future)
            except: pass
        
        for future in as_completed(futures):
            future.result()
    
    return domain_shells.get(base_url, [])

def scan_domain_fast(base_url):
    print(f"\n{'='*70}")
    print(f"⚡ FAST SCAN: {base_url}")
    print(f"{'='*70}")
    return scan_initial_paths_threaded(base_url, SCAN_PATHS)

def save_summary(all_results):
    total_threats = sum(len(shells) for shells in all_results.values())
    with open('shell_report.txt', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write("🕵️ OJS ULTRA FAST SCAN REPORT v16.7\n"+"="*50+"\n")
        f.write(f"Date: {time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S WIB')}\n")
        f.write(f"Total Domains: {len(all_results)}\nTotal Shells: {total_threats}\n\n")
        for domain, shells in all_results.items():
            f.write(f"🎯 {domain}: {len(shells)} shells\n")
            for shell in shells[:5]:
                rel_path = shell.replace(domain, '').lstrip('/')
                f.write(f"   → {rel_path}\n")
            f.write("\n")

def main():
    start_time = time.time()
    banner()
    
    domains = load_domains()
    if not domains: return
    
    print(f"\n🚀 ULTRA FAST SCAN: {len(domains)} domains [25 THREADS]\n")
    all_results = {}
    
    # ⚡ FAST DOMAIN SCANNING (5 concurrent domains)
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as domain_executor:
        domain_futures = {domain_executor.submit(scan_domain_fast, domain): domain for domain in domains}
        
        for future in as_completed(domain_futures):
            domain = domain_futures[future]
            shells = future.result()
            all_results[domain] = shells
            print(f"📊 {domain}: {len(shells)} shells")
    
    elapsed = time.time() - start_time
    print(f"\n{'='*70}")
    print(f"✅ COMPLETE: {elapsed:.1f}s")
    total_threats = sum(len(shells) for shells in all_results.values())
    print(f"🕵️  TOTAL SHELLS: {total_threats}")
    
    if total_threats > 0:
        print("\n🕵️  CRITICAL SHELLS!")
        save_summary(all_results)
        print("📄 shell_report.txt")
        send_telegram_alert(f"⚡ OJS Scan: {total_threats} SHELLS dari {len(domains)} domains!")
    else:
        print("\n✅ CLEAN!")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
